1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (9 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2>Vi er heldige – vi har to kilder med god kvalitet og kapasitet</h2>
Start your heading structure with h1
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h2 to h4

<h4 style="height: 80px; line-height: 1.2">Hva bør du gjøre hvis du får beskjed om å koke drikkevannet?</h4>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h3 instead of h4

<h4>Rapporter fra kildeovervåkning</h4>
Don't skip heading levels. Use h3 instead of h4

2.4.4 Formål med lenke (34 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link opens in new window without indication

Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link with href='#' and onclick should be a button

<a class="list-group-item print" data-placement="right" data-toggle="tooltip" href="#" onclick="window.print();" title="Skriv ut siden"><i class="fa fa-print fa-fw"></i><span>  Skriv ut</span></a>
Use <button> element for interactive controls, or add role='button'

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="search-text form-control" id="search-text" name="s" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>
4.1.1 Parsing (2 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.1 (4.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Duplicate ID found: 'page-header' appears 3 times

id="page-header"
Each ID must be unique on the page
Testregel 4.1.1 (4.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Duplicate ID found: 'content' appears 3 times

id="content"
Each ID must be unique on the page
4.1.2 Navn, rolle, verdi (2 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='navigation' needs an accessible name

<nav class="navbar navbar-top navbar-default navbar-fixed-top" role="navigation"> <div class="container-fluid"> <div class="navbar-wrapper"> <div class="navbar-header"> <button class="navbar-toggle" d
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='form' needs an accessible name

<form action="https://vestfoldvann.no/" class="search-form" id="search-form" method="get" role="form"> <div class="form-group"> <input class="search-text form-control" id="search-text" name="s" placeh
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="search-text form-control" id="search-text" name="s" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>
4.1.1 Parsing (2 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.1 (4.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Duplicate ID found: 'page-header' appears 11 times

id="page-header"
Each ID must be unique on the page
Testregel 4.1.1 (4.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

<a href="https://www.larvik.kommune.no/" target="_blank"> <img alt="" class="img-responsive" src="https://vestfoldvann.no/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/larvik-kommunevapen-icon.png"/> </a>
Add text content, aria-label, or image with alt text
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Link opens in new window without indication

<a href="http://4farger.no" target="_blank">4farger</a>
Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Link has no accessible name (empty link)

<a class="scrollup" href="#"><i class="fa fa-angle-double-up fa-4x"></i></a>
Add text content, aria-label, or image with alt text
3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="search-text form-control" id="search-text" name="s" placeholder="Søk" type="text" value=""/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>
4.1.2 Navn, rolle, verdi (2 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='navigation' needs an accessible name

<nav class="navbar navbar-top navbar-default navbar-fixed-top" role="navigation"> <div class="container-fluid"> <div class="navbar-wrapper"> <div class="navbar-header"> <button class="navbar-toggle" d
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='form' needs an accessible name

<form action="https://vestfoldvann.no/" class="search-form" id="search-form" method="get" role="form"> <div class="form-group"> <input class="search-text form-control" id="search-text" name="s" placeh
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
